name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr

info:Stayed in July 2021

info:1 Review
rating:4.5
posted:Posted July 28, 2021
msg:I recently returned home from a 2 night stay in this hotel. My stay was excellent and I thoroughly enjoyed it. The staff were friendly, helpful and approachable. They let me check in early as the room was ready to stay in. 
The hotels' facilities were modern and evidently well cared for. The best thing about the whole experience for me was the quality of the room; which was outstanding. 
The location is some distance away from the centre of Yueyang, but the city can be easily reached by taxi in around 20-30 minutes. The hotel is situated right on the edge of Dongting Lake which provides opportunities for walking and observing sunrise/sunset. 
The breakfast was varied and good quality. My only issue would be that the 'A la carte' menu didnt reflect what was actually available. Several items were not stocked so we had to ask a number of times to order food on a lunch/dinner time.
Overall, I thoroughly enjoyed my experience at this hotel and would recommend it to families, business people, friends, couples etc.

If you want to see the lake view at ordinary times, you can see some on the fourth floor. It is best to book an executive view room on the fifth floor or above. The breakfast is rich and replenished in time. It doesn't feel crowded even if it is full. The hotel's buffet dinner is not bad. The indoor swimming pool is good.
The disadvantage is that the underground parking lot cannot go directly to the room. You have to go to the lobby on the second floor first and then change the elevator, which is not very convenient. Ask the hotel for a children's toiletries set, and give adults toothpaste and toothbrush. The children's playground is too small, with nothing but slides, and no one to manage it. The hotel has relatively complete facilities, including a gym (small) and indoor and outdoor swimming pools. There are prompts for overseas swimming pools during renovation, reservation and check-in. The water in the indoor swimming pool is relatively clear.

Room:

Serve:
Front desk service is not bad. But there is basically no service at the pool. The Chinese restaurant closes at 8 o'clock for dinner. You can order Western food or order takeaway.

breakfast:

In fact, for some time before, I have been loyal to this brand, but some things made me stay away. I thought that Yueyang Pullman would be able to win a round this time, but it finally failed.
After getting on Didi from Yueyang East Station, a local driver had a brief chat with him, and he told me that this is the best hotel in Yueyang. I also verified this when I arrived at the hotel. Many weddings have been chosen here, which shows that the locals trust it.
Well, let's start with getting out of the car.
It was raining that night, and my friend and I were each carrying a suitcase. In addition to the rain, we were a little embarrassed. The friend was relatively thin. At this time, it seemed that dragging a suitcase was a bit bulky. When we were pulling our luggage and leaving the hotel gate, the concierge brother came to us. I thought he was here to help my friend with the luggage. When I was about to say "thank you", the little brother It was like seeing two ***, passing by us, yes, passing by lightly.
Next, check in and everything works fine. But when we dragged our luggage and walked into the room, the wonderful experience began. The fluffy catkins in the room, the curly human hair tissue in the corners, and the stubborn stains on the ground told me how many vicissitudes this room has experienced. Later, not only these places, but also the surface of desktops and indoor objects are full of surprises. We called the front desk, and the response was timely, because they sent the auntie in the linen room next door to handle the matter. The aunt's attitude is both apologetic and perfunctory. I can probably understand that the management may have shifted the responsibility for hygiene to the aunt. If poor hygiene is an established fact, the aunt may also have some punishment. But don't the management staff inspect the house after the aunt cleans it? In the end, I thought the way to deal with it was at least to change a room, because the check-in situation that night was not very full. But I didn‚Äôt expect my aunt to tell us that we need to clean and brush the floor again, no matter we checked in at almost 9 pm and need to rest, or whether it will affect the rest of other guests if we remember to clean the floor so late. How did you come up with this approach as an established hotel? ! In the end, I rejected this approach and it didn't matter. The most interesting thing came, the auntie said sorry, she wanted to give us a few more bottles of free mineral water! Haha, speechless.
One wave of ups and downs and another wave of ups and downs. When taking a shower in the bathroom, you can't squeeze out a drop of that big bottle of shower gel. empty! The floor drain was clogged, I don't know how many old things were piled in it, the water directly overflowed the water blocking stone, making the whole bathroom full of it.
The next day, when we left, we told the front desk about our experience, hoping they would take it seriously. The lady at the front desk apologized and wanted to give us 2 cans of Coke. I ---, no wonder the auntie gave us free mineral water. This is probably the tradition of Yueyang Pullman.
   Spring and Jingming are fortunately accompanied by the beautiful scenery of Yueyang Tower. Yueyang is a good place, but Yueyang Pullman is not. You have failed the Yueyang people's trust in you, and you have continued to give this brand less points for assists.
